    window.addEventListener("load", function () {
           window.cookieconsent.initialise({
           	"cookie": {
           		name:"attika_cookieconsent_dismissed"
           	},
 						"palette": {
 						    "popup": {
 						      "background": "#edeff5",
 						      "text": "#838391"
 						    },
 						    "button": {
 						      "background": "#4b81e8"
 						    }
 						 },
 						layout: "basic-header",
 						layouts: {
 						  'basic': '{{messagelink}}{{compliance}}',
 						  'basic-close': '{{messagelink}}{{compliance}}{{close}}',
 						  'basic-header': '{{header}}{{message}}{{link}}{{compliance}}',
 						  'no-link':'{{header}}{{message}}{{compliance}}',
 						},
 						"header": "test",							 							  
             "revokable": false,
             "position": "bottom",
             "autoOpen":true,
             "type": "info",
 					  "content": {
 					  	"header": "<div class='attika-logo' style='color:#fff;font-size: 1.5em;padding:0 10px 10px;'><em>Attika Reisen</em></div>",
 					    "message": m_cookiesText,
 					    "dismiss": m_cookiesAccept,
 					    "link": m_cookiesInfo,
 					    "href": "//www.attika.de/unternehmen/datenschutz/#cookies"
 					  },
 					  onPopupOpen: function(status) {
 					  					  						  		
 								function clearListCookies()
 								{   
 								    var cookies = document.cookie.split(";");
 								    for (var i = 0; i < cookies.length; i++)
 								    {   
 								        var spcook =  cookies[i].split("=");
 								        deleteCookie(spcook[0]);
 								    }
 								    function deleteCookie(cookiename)
 								    {
 								        var d = new Date();
 								        d.setDate(d.getDate() - 1);
 								        var expires = ";expires="+d;
 								        var name=cookiename;
 								        var value="";
 								        document.cookie = name + "=" + value + expires + "; path=/acc/html";                    
 								    }								    
 								}
 								
 								clearListCookies();						  		
 														  		
                 var type = this.options.type;
                 var didConsent = this.hasConsented();
                 var ccModal = document.getElementById("cc-modal");
                                  
                 if (type == 'opt-out' && !didConsent) {
                     gaOptout();
                    
                     if (this.options.revokable) {
                       
                         setTimeout(function () {
                             document.getElementsByClassName("cc-revoke")[0].style.display = "block";
                         });
                     }
                 }else if(didConsent){
                 	if(ccModal){
 		                setTimeout(function () {
 												ccModal.remove();                   			                  	                  			                    
 		                });
 		              }
 	                
 	                enablecookies();  	
                	                    	
                 }else if(!didConsent){
                 	if(ccModal){
 										setTimeout(function () {
 	
 									    var  name, arr;
 									    name = "show";
 									    arr = ccModal.className.split(" ");
 									    if (arr.indexOf(name) == -1) {
 									        ccModal.className += " " + name;
 									    }
 	
 	                  });
                   }
 								}
 														  
 					  },
 					  onInitialise: function(status) {
 					                	
                 var type = this.options.type;
                 var didConsent = this.hasConsented();
                 var ccModal = document.getElementById("cc-modal");                                
                                  
                 if (type == 'opt-out' && !didConsent) {
                     gaOptout();
                    
                     if (this.options.revokable) {
                       
                         setTimeout(function () {
                             document.getElementsByClassName("cc-revoke")[0].style.display = "block";
                         });
                     }
                 }else if(didConsent){
                 	if(ccModal){
 		                setTimeout(function () {
 		                  	var ccModal = document.getElementById("cc-modal");
 												if(ccModal) ccModal.remove();                   			                  	                  			                    
 		                });
 		              }
 	                enablecookies();  	
                	                    	
                 }else if(!didConsent){
                 	if(ccModal){
 										setTimeout(function () {
 	
 									    var element, name, arr;
 									    element = document.getElementById("cc-modal");
 									    name = "show";
 									    arr = element.className.split(" ");
 									    if (arr.indexOf(name) == -1) {
 									        element.className += " " + name;
 									    }
 	
 	                  });
 									}                  
 								}                    
 					  
 					  },						  
             onStatusChange: function (status, chosenBefore) {
                 var type = this.options.type;                
                 var didConsent = this.hasConsented();
                 var ccModal = document.getElementById("cc-modal");
                                    
                 if (type == 'opt-out' && !didConsent) {
                     gaOptout();
                 }
                 if (type == 'opt-out' && didConsent) {
                     //enable cookies
                     enablecookies();
                 }else if(didConsent){
                 	enablecookies();
                 	if(ccModal)
                 		$('#cc-modal').fadeOut(250,function(){$(this).remove();});
                 }
             }
              
           });
       });
 
     	function enablecookies(){      	
 				/* Google Analytics */					
 				(function(i,s,o,g,r,a,m){i['GoogleAnalyticsObject']=r;i[r]=i[r]||function(){
 				(i[r].q=i[r].q||[]).push(arguments)},i[r].l=1*new Date();a=s.createElement(o),
 				m=s.getElementsByTagName(o)[0];a.async=1;a.src=g;m.parentNode.insertBefore(a,m)
 				})(window,document,'script','//www.google-analytics.com/analytics.js','ga');
 				
 				ga('create', 'UA-25623768-1', 'auto');
 				ga('send', 'pageview');
 				ga('set', 'anonymizeIp', true);
 									
 				<!-- Facebook Pixel Code -->
 				!function(f,b,e,v,n,t,s){if(f.fbq)return;n=f.fbq=function(){n.callMethod?
 				n.callMethod.apply(n,arguments):n.queue.push(arguments)};if(!f._fbq)f._fbq=n;
 				n.push=n;n.loaded=!0;n.version='2.0';n.queue=[];t=b.createElement(e);t.async=!0;
 				t.src=v;s=b.getElementsByTagName(e)[0];s.parentNode.insertBefore(t,s)}(window,
 				document,'script','https://connect.facebook.net/en_US/fbevents.js');
 				fbq('init', '1865426157054472');
 				fbq('track', 'PageView');
 				<!-- DO NOT MODIFY -->
 				<!-- End Facebook Pixel Code -->						
 			}
 			
 			
 			/* Google Analytics Optout - Optin */
 			var gaProperty = 'UA-25623768-1';
 			var disableStr = 'ga-disable-' + gaProperty;
 			if (document.cookie.indexOf(disableStr + '=true') > -1) {
 				window[disableStr] = true;
 			}				
 								
 			function gaOptout() {
 			
 				var res = confirm(gaOptoutConfirm);
 				if (res) {
 				  document.cookie = disableStr + '=true; expires=Thu, 31 Dec 2099 23:59:59 UTC; path=/';
 				  window[disableStr] = true;
 				  alert(gaOptoutSuccess);
 				}
 			
 			}
 			
 			function gaOptin() {
 			
 				var res = confirm(gaOptinConfirm);
 				if (res) {
 				  document.cookie = disableStr + '=false; expires=Thu, 31 Dec 2099 23:59:59 UTC; path=/';
 				  window[disableStr] = false;
 				  alert(gaOptinSuccess);
 				}
 			
 			}

 		// GET URL Variablen als (ass.) array zurueckgeben.
 		function getUrlVars() {
 		   var vars = [], hash;
 		   var hashes = window.location.href.slice(window.location.href.indexOf('?') + 1).split('&');
 		   for(var i = 0; i < hashes.length; i++) {
 		       hash = hashes[i].split('=');
 		       vars.push(hash[0]);
 		       vars[hash[0]] = hash[1];
 		   }
 		   return vars;
 		}
 				
 		function getDateSelected(){
 							
 			var dateSelected = [];
 					
 			var start, end;
 									
 			if(!erwLoaded || !$('#daterange').length){
 								var rtage = 7;
 				start = new Date();
 				end = start.setDate(start.getDate() + rtage);
 				start = moment.utc(start).utc();
 				end = moment.utc(end).utc();
 				
 							}else{
 				start = moment.utc($('#daterange').data('daterangepicker').startDate.format('YYYY-MM-DDTHH:mm:ss') + 'Z').utc();
 				end   = moment.utc($('#daterange').data('daterangepicker').endDate.format('YYYY-MM-DDTHH:mm:ss') + 'Z').utc();															
 			}
 						
 			dateSelected['start'] = Date.UTC(parseInt(start.format('YYYY')),parseInt(start.format('M'))-1,parseInt(start.format('D')),0,0,0,0);
 			dateSelected['end']   = Date.UTC(parseInt(end.format('YYYY')),parseInt(end.format('M'))-1,parseInt(end.format('D')),0,0,0,0);
 			dateSelected['dateStart'] = new Date(start.format('YYYY-MM-DD')+'T00:00:00');
 			dateSelected['dateEnd'] = new Date(end.format('YYYY-MM-DD')+'T00:00:00');
 						
 			return dateSelected;
 		}
 		
 		var changingType = true;	
 					
 		var lastType = '';
 		
 		// set search buttons state (pauschal/selbstsanreise/nur Flüg)
 		function setTypeOfSearch(type){
 												
 			if(ajaxManager.requests.length>0 && type!='rooms_avail')
 				ajaxManager.abort();
 					
 			var drp = $('#daterange').data('daterangepicker');
 					
 			$(".nav.type-search > li").removeClass("active");
 			$("#"+type).parent().addClass("active");
 			
 			if(type!='only_mietwagen' && !isHotelPage){
 				$('.afhsel-wrapper').removeClass('hide');
 				$('.zfhsel-wrapper').removeClass('hide');
 				$('.perssel-wrapper').removeClass('hide');
 				$('.rcasel-wrapper').addClass('hide');
 				$('input[name="rca"]:checked').prop('checked',false);
 				$('#rcasel').val('');
 				$('.rcasel-wrapper').next().removeClass('col-md-4').removeClass('col-sm-6').addClass('col-md-3').addClass('col-sm-4');
 				$('#submitbutton').closest('.col-xs-12').removeClass('col-md-3').addClass('col-md-2');
 			}
 
 			if(type=='s' || type=='p'){			
         if(!$('#zfh-all').is(':checked') && $('#zfhopts input:radio[name="zfh"]:checked').length>0 && btyp!='x'){
         	$('#cb-mainlocations').removeClass('hide');
         	$('#cb-mainlocations').trigger('changedDestination');
         }
 			}
 											
 			switch(type){
 				case 'rooms_avail':
 								
 					if($('.avail-header').is(':hidden')){
 						$('.avail-header').removeClass('hide').addClass('row-active');
 					}else{
 						$('.avail-header').trigger('click');
 					}
 										
 					$('#rooms_avail').parent('li').removeClass('active');
 					
 					if(lastType=='s')
 						$('#only_hotel').parent('li').addClass('active');
 					else
 						$('#flight_hotel').parent('li').addClass('active');
 					
 					if($('.avail-container').is(':hidden'))		
 						$('#rooms_avail').parent('li').removeClass('selected');							
 					else{
 						$('#rooms_avail').parent('li').addClass('selected');
 						$('.box-content').redraw();
 					}
 					
 					$('#avail_text .to-hotel-top').trigger('click');
 										
 					break;						
 					
 				case 'only_hotel':
 						
 					$('#afh-self').closest('li').show();
 					$('#zfh-all').closest('li').show();
 														
 					if(isHotelPage)
 						$("#afhsel").closest('.afhsel-wrapper').children().first().hide();
 																			
 					if(lastType=='p' && $('input[name="afh"]:checked').length>0 && !$('#afh-self:checked').lenght>0 && !isHotelPage){
 						setTypeOfSearch('flight_hotel');
 						break;
 					}
 					
 					btyp = 's';
 					
 					$('input[name="only"]').val(btyp);				
 									
 					// coming from flight tab
 					if(!isHotelPage){
 						
 						$('input[name="afh"]:checked').each(function(){
 											
 							if(!$(this).is('#afh-self'))
 								$(this).prop('checked',false);
 							
 						});
 						
 					}								
 					
 					if(isSearchPage)
 						$(".nav-search").removeClass("hide");
 												
 					changingType = true;				
 									
 					//$("#self").prop("checked",true);
 					$("#pau").prop("checked",false);				
 					$("#plusmin-sel").val("0").change();
 									
 					$("input[name='only']").val("s");
 					$("input[name='mdf']").val("SGAL");
 					//$("#afhsel").val(m_sHotelOnly);				
 					//$("input[type=\'radio\'][name=\'afh\']:checked").prop("checked",false);
 					//$("#afh-self").prop("checked",true);
 					
 					$('input[name="afhs"]').val('');								
 					
 					if($("#zfhsel").val()==''){
 																	
 						$("#zfhsel").val("");
 					}
 													
 					if($("input[type=\'radio\'][name=\'zfh\']:checked").length>0){
 						$zfh_checked = $("input[type=\'radio\'][name=\'zfh\']:checked");
 						if(!isHotelPage){
 							$("#zfhsel").val($zfh_checked.parent('label').find('span').text());
 							$zfh_checked.change();
 						}
 					}											
 													
 					if(erwLoaded && !isHotelPage){
 						$('#erw_suches').removeClass('disabled');
 						$('.main-attributes').fadeIn();
 						$('.attributes-housing').fadeIn();	
 					}				
 					                  
 	        if(drp!==undefined){
 	        	drp.wts = '';
 	        	$('.range_inputs').find('.img-square-10').addClass('hide').removeClass('show').next('span').addClass('hide').removeClass('show');	
 	        };
 	        
 	        if(isHotelPage){
 	        	$('#low-hot-text').removeClass('hide').addClass('show');
 	        	$('#transfer-text').removeClass('show').addClass('hide');	
 	        }
 	        	
 	        if(isSearchPage && $('#cb-sorting').is(':hidden'))
 	        	$('#cb-sorting').fadeIn();	
 					
 					changingType = false;
 	
 					updateAttributes('#'+type);
 					
 					lastType = 's';
 					
 					break;
 				case 'only_flight':
 					changingType = true;
 					
 					btyp = 'x';
 										
 					$('input[name="only"]').val(btyp);
 										
 					if(isSearchPage && erwLoaded){
 						$(".inhalt").empty();
 						$('input[name="showmap"]').val('0');	
 					}								
 									
 					if($('#afh-self').is(':checked')){						
 						$('#afh-self').prop('checked',false).change();
 					}
 	
 					if($('#zfh-all').is(':checked')){
 						$('#zfh-all').prop('checked',false);
 						$("#zfhsel").val('');
 					}								
 									
 					$('#afh-self').closest('li').hide();
 					$('#zfh-all').closest('li').hide();
 					
 					if(!$('#cb-mainlocations').hasClass('hide'))
 						$('#cb-mainlocations').addClass('hide');									
 									
 					if(isHotelPage){
 						$("#afhsel").closest('.afhsel-wrapper').children().first().show();
 						$("#afhsel").focus();
 					}
 																	
 					if(isSearchPage)
 						$(".nav-search").addClass("hide");
 					
 					$("#pau").prop("checked",false);
 					$("#self").prop("checked",false);
 					$("#pauself").prop("checked",false).change();
 					$("#plusmin-sel").val("3").change();
 				
 					if(erwLoaded){
 						removeAttributes();
 					}				
 					$('#erw_suches').addClass('disabled');
 					$('.main-attributes').hide();
 					$('.attributes-housing').hide();
 					$("input[name='only']").val("x");
 					$("input[name='mdf']").val("");
 					$("#afhsel").prop("disabled",false);				
 					if($("#afhsel").val()==''|| $('#afhsel').val()==$('#afhsel').prop('defaultValue') || $('#afhsel').val()=='Abflughafen'){
 						 //added				
 												if(abflughafen==''){
 							$("#afhsel").val('');
 						}
 					}
 					
 					if($('#afhopts .popopt:checked').length>0){
 						if(!erwLoaded){
 													
 							var selAips = '';
 							var afhs    = '';
 							
 							if(selAips=='' && $('#afhopts .popopt:checked').length){
 								$('#afhopts .popopt:checked').each(function(){
 									afhs += $(this).val();
 								});
 								$('input[name="afhs"]').val(afhs);										
 							}
 														
 							if ($('#afhopts .popopt:checked').length==1)
 								$('#afhsel').val($('#afhopts .popopt:checked').parent('label').find('span').text());
 							else
 								$('#afhsel').val($('#afhopts .popopt:checked').length+' Abflughäfen');
 																																					
 						}else{
 												
 							$('#afhsel').val('');
 							$('input[name="afhs"]').val('');
 							
 							var _lastType = lastType;
 												
 							$('#afhopts .popopt:checked').each(function(){
 													
 								$(this).change();
 																						
 							});
 							
 							lastType = _lastType;
 	
 						}										
 											
 					}else{
 					
 						$('#afhsel').val('');
 						$('input[name="afhs"]').val('');
 	
 					}												
 																									
 					if($("#zfhsel").val()==''){
 										
 						$("#zfhsel").val("").change();													
 					}				
 	
 					if($("input[type=\'radio\'][name=\'zfh\']:checked").length>0 && erwLoaded){				
 						$zfh_checked = $("input[type=\'radio\'][name=\'zfh\']:checked");
 						$zfh_checked.prop("checked",true);			
 						if(!isHotelPage) $zfh_checked.trigger("change");
 					}
 																						
 	        if(isHotelPage){
 	        	$('#low-hot-text').removeClass('show').addClass('hide');
 	        	$('#transfer-text').removeClass('hide').addClass('hide');
 	        }
 	        	
 	        if(isSearchPage && $('#cb-sorting').is(':hidden'))
 	        	$('#cb-sorting').hide();	        	
 	        	
 	        if(drp!==undefined){
 	        	$('.range_inputs').find('.img-square-10').addClass('show').removeClass('hide').next('span').addClass('show').removeClass('hide');	
 	        };				
 				
 					changingType = false;
 																		
 					updateAttributes('_none_');
 					
 					if(hotelRemoved) hotelRemoved = false;
 					
 					if(isSearchPage && isFormValidated()){
 						$('#submitbutton').trigger('click');
 					}								
 									
 					break;
 				case 'only_mietwagen':
 					changingType = true;
 					
 					btyp = 'm';
 					
 					$('input[name="only"]').val(btyp);								
 																	
 					if(isSearchPage)
 						$(".nav-search").addClass("hide");
 					
 					if(isSearchPage && erwLoaded){
 						$(".inhalt").empty();
 						$('input[name="showmap"]').val('0');
 					}												
 					
 					$("#plusmin-sel").val("0").change();
 				
 					if(erwLoaded){
 						removeAttributes();
 					}
 					
 					$('.afhsel-wrapper').addClass('hide');
 					$('.zfhsel-wrapper').addClass('hide');				
 					$('.perssel-wrapper').addClass('hide');
 					$('.rcasel-wrapper').removeClass('hide');
 					
 					$('.rcasel-wrapper').next().removeClass('col-md-3').removeClass('col-sm-4').addClass('col-md-4').addClass('col-sm-6');
 					$('#submitbutton').closest('.col-xs-12').removeClass('col-md-2').addClass('col-md-3');
 									
 					$('#erw_suches').addClass('disabled');
 					$('.main-attributes').hide();
 					$('.attributes-housing').hide();
 					
 					$("input[name='only']").val('m');
 					$("input[name='mdf']").val('');
 					$('input[name="afhs"]').val('');
 													
 					$("#pau").prop("checked", false);
 					$("#self").prop("checked",false);
 					
 					changingType = false;
 					
 					if(isSearchPage && $('input[name="rca"]:checked').length>0){
 						$('input[name="rca"]:checked').change();
 						updateAttributes('#'+type);
 					}
 													
 					break;				
 				default:
 					changingType = true;
 										
 					btyp = 'p';
 										
 					$('input[name="only"]').val(btyp);												
 																	
 					if(isHotelPage){
 						$("#afhsel").closest('.afhsel-wrapper').children().first().show();
 						$("#afhsel").focus();
 						$("#flight_hotel").parent().addClass("active");				
 					}else{
 						$("#only_hotel").parent().addClass("active");
 					}
 														
 					if(isSearchPage)
 						$(".nav-search").removeClass("hide");				
 									
 					$("#pau").prop("checked", true);
 					$("#self").prop("checked",false);
 					$("#plusmin-sel").val("3").change();				
 					
 					$("input[name='only']").val("p");
 					$("input[name='mdf']").val("PGAL");
 					$("#afhsel").removeProp("disabled");
 					$("#afhsel").css("background-color", "#fff");
 					if($("#afhsel").val()==''|| $('#afhsel').val()==$('#afhsel').prop('defaultValue') || $('#afhsel').val()==''){
 						 //added
 												if(abflughafen=='' || $("input[name='afh'][value='']").length===0)
 							$("#afhsel").val('');
 					}
 													
 					if($('#afhopts .popopt:checked').length>0){						
 						if(!erwLoaded){					
 							
 							if ($('#afhopts .popopt:checked').length==1)
 								$('#afhsel').val($('#afhopts .popopt:checked').parent('label').find('span').text());
 							else
 								$('#afhsel').val($('#afhopts .popopt:checked').length+' Abflughäfen');
 																													
 						}else{
 						
 							$('#afhsel').val('');
 							$('input[name="afhs"]').val('');
 							
 							var _lastType = lastType;
 												
 							$('#afhopts .popopt:checked').each(function(){
 													
 								$(this).change();
 																						
 							});
 							
 							lastType = _lastType;
 	
 						}										
 											
 					}else{
 					
 						$('#afhsel').val('');
 						$('input[name="afhs"]').val('');
 	
 					}												
 																									
 					if($("#zfhsel").val()==''){
 										
 						$("#zfhsel").val("").change();													
 					}				
 	
 					if($("input[type=\'radio\'][name=\'zfh\']:checked").length>0 && erwLoaded){				
 						$zfh_checked = $("input[type=\'radio\'][name=\'zfh\']:checked");
 						$zfh_checked.prop("checked",true);			
 						if(!isHotelPage) $zfh_checked.trigger("change");
 					}
 													
 					if(erwLoaded && !isHotelPage){
 						$('#erw_suches').removeClass('disabled');
 						$('.main-attributes').fadeIn();
 						$('.attributes-housing').fadeIn();	
 					}
 									
 	        if(isHotelPage){
 	        	$('#low-hot-text').removeClass('show').addClass('hide');
 	        	$('#transfer-text').removeClass('hide').addClass('show');
 	        }
 	        	
 	        if(isSearchPage && $('#cb-sorting').is(':hidden'))
 	        	$('#cb-sorting').fadeIn();	        	
 	        	
 	        if(drp!==undefined){
 	        	$('.range_inputs').find('.img-square-10').addClass('show').removeClass('hide').next('span').addClass('show').removeClass('hide');	
 	        };				
 				
 					changingType = false;
 																		
 					updateAttributes('#'+type);
 					
 					lastType='p';
 									
 					break;
 									
 				}
 				
 				if(!erwLoaded)
 						lastAvailCheck = btyp;
 																							
 		}
 		
 		/* Begin Cookie Consent plugin by Silktide - http://silktide.com/cookieconsent */
 		//	window.cookieconsent_options = {"message":"<span class='attika-logo' style='color:#fff;font-size: 1.2em;'><em>Attika Reisen</em></span>&nbsp;&nbsp;verwendet Cookies, um Ihr Erlebnis auf unserer Website zu verbessern. Wenn Sie die Website weiter nutzen, stimmen Sie der Verwendung von Cookies zu.&nbsp;","dismiss":"Akzeptieren","learnMore":"Mehr Info","link":"unternehmen/datenschutz/?#cookies","theme":"dark-bottom"};
 		/* End Cookie Consent plugin */
   </script>

 $(function() {  $('#daterange').daterangepicker({  "locale": {  "language": 'de'  }, 	"wts": '', "showDropdowns": true,  "startDate": '22-08-2018',  "endDate": '29-08-2018',  "minDate": '05-08-2018',  "opens": 'center'  }); /* daterangepicker() */	if(typeof $('#daterange').data('daterangepicker')!=="undefined"){	var start =  moment(($('#daterange').data('daterangepicker').startDate));  $('#tag').val(start.format('DD'));  $('#mon').val(start.format('MM'));  $('#jahr').val(start.format('YYYY'));  if($("#afhsel").val()!=$("#afhsel").prop("defaultValue")) {$("#afhsel").parent().find('.popopt:checked').trigger("change");}  if($("#zfhsel").val()!=$("#zfhsel").prop("defaultValue")) {$("#zfhsel").parent().find('.popopt:checked').trigger("change");}}$('#daterange').on('apply.daterangepicker', function(ev, picker) {	var startDate =  moment(($('#daterange').data('daterangepicker').startDate));	var endDate		=  moment(($('#daterange').data('daterangepicker').endDate));  var sDate = moment(startDate,'DD-MM-YYYY');  var eDate = moment(endDate,'DD-MM-YYYY');  $('#tag').val(startDate.format('DD'));  $('#mon').val(startDate.format('MM'));  $('#jahr').val(startDate.format('YYYY'));  $('#reisetage').val(eDate.diff(sDate,'days'));  if(isHotelPage){	  var oldStartDate =  moment(($('#daterange').data('daterangepicker').oldStartDate));	  var oldEndDate   =  moment(($('#daterange').data('daterangepicker').oldEndDate));    if(startDate._d.getTime()!=oldStartDate._d.getTime() || endDate._d.getTime()!=oldEndDate._d.getTime())      updateAttributes('#'+$(this).prop('id'));  }});$(".daterangepicker").addClass("show-calendar");if($('input[name="afh"]').is(":checked") && $('input[name="zfh"]').is(":checked")) $('input[name="afh"]').trigger("change"); $("#plusmin-sel").val("0");$("#plusmin-sel").on("change", function(){	$("input[name='pm']").val($(this).val());});});
